style="font-family:Arial;font-size:11pt;font-weight:bold;">WINNEBAGO INDUSTRIES ANNOUNCES THIRD QUARTER FISCAL 2019 RESULTS</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Sales Performance Continues to Outperform RV and Marine Industries --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Quarterly Gross Margins of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">16.4%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;Basis Points Over Prior Year --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Quarterly Diluted EPS of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">$1.14</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">, Up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">12%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;Over Prior Year --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">-- Strong YTD Operating Cash Flow, Up 36% Over Prior Year --</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">FOREST CITY, IOWA, </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">June&#160;19, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;- Winnebago Industries, Inc. (NYSE:WGO), a leading outdoor lifestyle product manufacturer, today reported financial results for the Company's Fiscal 2019 </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">&#32;Quarter Results</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Revenues for the Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter ended </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">May&#160;25, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$528.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, a decrease of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">5.9%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$562.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2018</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;period. Gross profit was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$86.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">1.3%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$85.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2018</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;period. Gross profit margin increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">120</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;basis points in the quarter, driven by continued strong margin performance in the Towable segment. Operating income was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$49.0 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the quarter, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">1.4%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$48.3 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;in the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter of last year, and was unfavorably impacted by the restructuring costs associated with moving our diesel manufacturing from Junction City, Oregon to Northern Iowa, totaling $1.1 million, or $0.03 diluted earnings per share. Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter net income was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$36.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">11.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$32.5 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;in the same period last year. Earnings per diluted share were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$1.14</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">11.8%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;compared to earnings per diluted share of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$1.02</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;in the same period last year. Net income and earnings per share were favorably impacted by an improved tax rate resulting from the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act ("TCJA"), totaling $1.7 million, or $0.06 diluted earnings per share, and a change in estimate related to R&amp;D tax credits of $1.4 million, or $0.04 diluted earnings per share. Consolidated Adjusted EBITDA was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$55.9 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the quarter, compared to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$53.4 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;last year, resulting in an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">4.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">President and Chief Executive Officer Michael Happe commented, &#8220;We are pleased to deliver another quarter of solid consolidated results highlighted by continued margin expansion and market share gains. Winnebago Industries&#8217; third quarter results are a testament to the strength and resiliency of our brand portfolio amid a challenging and highly competitive RV market. We continue to focus on manufacturing high-quality products, maintaining disciplined production management and enhancing channel relationships. Despite a moderate decrease in overall sales in a difficult RV wholesale market, consolidated margin continued to expand, primarily due to the strength of our dual-branded Towable segment. We continue to be pleased with our strengthened market position as we outperform the industries in which we compete. I want to thank all of our Winnebago Industries employees for their dedication to making the Company a trusted leader in outdoor lifestyle solutions. Their hard work and flexibility during the quarter is appreciated as we continued to manage output during these past several months of marketplace volatility.&#8221; </font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">1</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><br></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Motorhome</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">In the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter, revenues for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Motorhome</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;segment were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$160.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, down </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">34.6%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;from the prior year driven by decreases in both Class C and Class A unit sales as dealers continue to lower their inventories. Class B unit sales and Motorhome segment profitability were also down versus the prior year due to a temporary, but material, disruption in chassis supply by one of our strategic suppliers, which had a significant impact on shipment availability for two of our most popular Class B units. Supply is improving during the early part of our fourth quarter, and we expect our Class B portfolio to return to strong performance in the back half of our fourth quarter and during Fiscal 2020. Despite these headwinds, our retail performance in the Class B category has remained robust. Segment Adjusted EBITDA was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$0.4 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, down </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">96.7%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;from the prior year. Adjusted EBITDA margin decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">460</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;basis points, driven primarily by deleverage, an unfavorable mix due to the decline in sales of our most profitable products, and continued discounting in the marketplace. Backlog decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">5.6%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, in dollars, compared to the prior year reflecting dealers efforts to right-size inventory levels, partially offset by an increase in several Class B products due to the temporary disruption in chassis supply.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Towable</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Revenues for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Towable</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;segment were </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$346.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">10.8%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;from the prior year, driven particularly by the strength of the Grand Design RV brand. Segment Adjusted EBITDA was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$57.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, up </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">26.0%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;over the prior year. Adjusted EBITDA margin of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">16.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;increased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">200</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;basis points, reflecting an increase in unit sales, pricing actions taken over the past twelve months, and effectively managing input cost pressures. Backlog decreased </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">24.2%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, in dollars, compared to the prior year, reflecting the positive impact of utilizing additional capacity added during calendar 2018 and dealers continuing to normalize inventory levels.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Tax</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Our effective tax rate for the third quarter was 19.4%, driven lower by the year-over-year impact of the reduction in the corporate income tax rate associated with the TCJA and a favorable change in estimate related to R&amp;D tax credits. The impact from the TCJA and change in estimate was $0.06 and $0.04 to diluted earnings per share, respectively. Considering our year-to-date tax provision, including all favorable discrete items and changes in estimates, as well as our current ongoing tax rate assumptions for the remainder of the year, we expect our full year Fiscal 2019 tax rate to be approximately 20%, before consideration of any discrete tax items in our fourth quarter. Under the current tax code, we expect our ongoing tax rate in Fiscal 2020 and beyond to be in the range of 23% to 24%, before consideration of any discrete tax items.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Balance Sheet and Cash Flow</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">As of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">May&#160;25, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, the Company had total outstanding debt of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$259.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;(</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$265.6 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;of debt, net of debt issuance costs of $6.0 million) and working capital of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$186.2 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">. The debt-to-equity ratio decreased to </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">43.0%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;from </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">54.5%</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;as of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">August&#160;25, 2018</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, and the ratio of net debt to Adjusted EBITDA was 1.4x as of the end of the quarter. Cash flow from operations was </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$82.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;for the first </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">nine</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;months of Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, an increase of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$21.8 million</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;from the same period in Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2018</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Quarterly Cash Dividend</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">On </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">May 22, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, the Company&#8217;s board of directors approved a quarterly cash dividend of </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">$0.11</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;per share payable on </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">July 3, 2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">, to common stockholders of record at the close of business on </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Mr. Happe continued, &#8220;As we transition into the final quarter of Fiscal 2019, we are well positioned to continue our positive momentum with top line sales and share gains. Our North American RV retail share is approaching 10%, up from 3% just three years ago. The imbalance between industry wholesale shipments and retail sales continues to improve and will continue to do so in the back half of calendar 2019. The materials cost environment remains volatile, as newly implemented and pending tariffs start to impact cost inputs in the back half of calendar 2019. We absorbed an unexpected challenge to our motorhome sales and </font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div><br></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">profits during the quarter due primarily to a supply interruption of Class B chassis and we remain focused on seeing that situation improve. We are pleased with the recent pace of steady inbound RV orders from dealers. Additionally, Chris-Craft has launched several new models in the front half of 2019, which will continue their momentum forward in the marine industry. Our broader portfolio, combined with our operational resiliency as a company, are working to solidify our unique position within the outdoor lifestyle market and making Winnebago Industries a high-quality company that investors can trust to deliver value.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">Conference Call</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Winnebago Industries, Inc. will discuss </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">third</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;quarter Fiscal </font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">2019</font><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">&#32;earnings results during a conference call scheduled for 9:00 a.m. Central Time today. Members of the news media, investors and the general public are invited to access a live broadcast of the conference call via the Investor Relations page of the Company's website at http://investor.wgo.net. The event will be archived and available for replay for the next 90 days.</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;text-decoration:underline;">About Winnebago Industries</font></div><div style="line-height:174%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Winnebago Industries, Inc. is a leading U.S. manufacturer of outdoor lifestyle products under the Winnebago, Grand Design, and Chris-Craft brands, which are used primarily in leisure travel and outdoor recreation activities. The Company builds quality motorhomes, travel trailers, fifth wheel products, and boats. Winnebago Industries has multiple facilities in Iowa, Indiana, Minnesota, and Florida. The Company's common stock is listed on the New York Stock Exchange and traded under the symbol WGO. style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">We have provided non-GAAP performance measures of EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA as a comparable measure to illustrate the effect of non-recurring transactions occurring during the reported periods and improve comparability of our results from period to period. EBITDA is defined as net income before interest expense, provision for income taxes, and depreciation and amortization expense. Adjusted EBITDA is defined as net income before interest expense, provision for income taxes, depreciation and amortization expense, and other adjustments made in order to present comparable results from period to period. We believe Adjusted EBITDA provides meaningful supplemental information about our operating performance because this measure excludes amounts that we do not consider part of our core operating results when assessing our performance. Examples of items excluded from Adjusted EBITDA include acquisition-related costs, restructuring expenses, and non-operating income.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">Management uses these non-GAAP financial measures (a)&#160;to evaluate its historical and prospective financial performance and trends as well as its performance relative to competitors and peers; (b)&#160;to measure operational profitability on a consistent basis; (c) in presentations to the members of its board of directors to enable its board of directors to have the same measurement basis of operating performance as is used by management in their assessments of performance and in forecasting and budgeting for our company; (d) to evaluate potential acquisitions; and, (e) to ensure compliance with covenants and restricted activities under the terms of its Credit Agreement. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are frequently used by securities analysts, investors, and other interested parties to evaluate companies in our industry.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;">9</font></div></div>	</body>
